          function checkSubmit(e) {
                        var keycode;
                        if (window.event)
                            keycode = window.event.keyCode;
                        else if (e)
                            keycode = e.which;
                        else
                            return true;

                        if (keycode == 13) {
                            document.form1.submit();
                            return false;
                        } else {
                            return true;
                        }
                    }
                    function focusPassword(e) {
                        var keycode;
                        if (window.event)
                            keycode = window.event.keyCode;
                        else if (e)
                            keycode = e.which;
                        else
                            return true;

                        if (keycode == 13) {
                            //document.form1.password.focus();
                            return false;
                        }
                        return true;
                    }
